additionalURL = paramsArray[1];             var urlParamDelimiter = "";             if (additionalURL) {                 paramsArray = additionalURL.split("&");                 var arrayLength = paramsArray.length;                 for (var i = 0; i < arrayLength; i++){                     if(paramsArray[i].split("=")[0] != param){                         newAdditionalURL += urlParamDelimiter + paramsArray[i];                         urlParamDelimiter = "&";                     }                 }             }              var modifiedParam = urlParamDelimiter + "" + param + "=" + paramVal;             return baseURL + "?" + newAdditionalURL + modifiedParam;         }                  function getIFrameHeight(){             var avail =  A.viewport().height - 300; Robe features thick, 15 ounce polar fleece fabric that is extremely soft and lightweight, yet has a high insulating ability. Wrap around waist tie and double belt loops make for a custom fit. Two wide front pockets and roll up cuff sleeves add to the comfort of this robe. Inactive dyes used (chemical free).  Superior quality.  If you're not completely satisfied with this bathrobe returns are accepted.<p><b>Washing Instructions:</b> <br />Wash in cool water with like colors.  Dry on low heat only.<p><b>Sizing Recommendations:</b> <br />Small/Medium: Will fit Chests 34-40 inches, Robe length 48 inches<br />Large/XL: Will fit Chests 42-48 inches, Robe length 48<br />1XL/2XL: Will fit Chests 48-52 inches, Robe length 57 inches<br />3XL-4XL: Will fit Chests 54-60 inches, Robe length 58 inches<br /></p>                                                        </div> id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R33UN1BBFLQIJN" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">     Verified Purchase   </span>      <div class="a-section">   The robe is very soft, comfortable, and certainly fits my well enough.  I ordered the XL-XXL version, and it fits my XXL frame very well.  My only issues so far are these:  It is a cat hair magnet.  Also, the gentleman in the picture is probably 8 feet tall.  I am 6'0", and the robe goes all the way down to my ankles and lower.  When I walk up or down stairs, I need to be very careful to not trip.  So, when you buy this robe know that it is a LOT longer than the image seems to convey. </div>  </div>        <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="1"
